    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText14037710692490607504" style="display:none">I couldn't put this book down. It is about Nikki Maxwell. She is in danger of having to leave the school again. This time it is because of Mackenzie. Nikki toilet papered Mackenzie's house because Mackenzie is a witch. Mackenzie threatened to tell the principal and get Chloe, Zoey, and Nikki thrown out of school. Another reason she might have to leave is because she attends the school on a bug extermination scholarship. Her dad started working for Mackenzie's dad and might work full time. To make sure Mackenzie doesn't put any thing in the newspaper she joins the school newspaper team. Mackenzie is off to her tricks again though, she scribbled Nikki's name off the sign up sheet. Mr.Zimmerman won't talk to Nikki about this. Eventually he gives her the job of Miss-Know-it-All. This is the advice column of the newspaper. The first day of checking the advice boxes the only thing that was in them was trash. But in the end there are over two hundred notes a day. Nikki needs to find Brandon, her crush a birthday present. She goes to the mall, but spends all her money on her sister and her self. The party is getting closer and she still doesn't have a present. Will she get the present? Can she keep up with the advice letters? Read to find out! I recommend this book to any tween girl. It was amazing, and the illustrations were hilarious. I love Dork Diaries. I am totally a dork!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer493778217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1768385926663675611">4.5 stars<br/><br/>Nikki is at a sleepover with her friends Chloe, and Zoey. They play truth or dare, and to avoid answering questions about Brandon, Nikki chooses a dare. She is dared to toilet paper Mackenzie Hollister house, a CCP girl that she can't stand. At first, she doesn't want to, but then thinks about all the mean things that Mackenzie has done to her and her friends.<br/><br/>They all go and toilet paper her house, and Mackenzie catches them before they can leave. However, Mackenzie is convinced that Br</span>
  <span id="freeText1768385926663675611" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />Nikki is at a sleepover with her friends Chloe, and Zoey. They play truth or dare, and to avoid answering questions about Brandon, Nikki chooses a dare. She is dared to toilet paper Mackenzie Hollister house, a CCP girl that she can't stand. At first, she doesn't want to, but then thinks about all the mean things that Mackenzie has done to her and her friends.<br /><br />They all go and toilet paper her house, and Mackenzie catches them before they can leave. However, Mackenzie is convinced that Brandon, Nikki's crush, did it because he's crushing at her. Nikki and her friends can't believe they are getting away with it.<br /><br />Mackenzie is furious when she isn't invited to Brandon's party but Nikki and her friends are invited. Mackenzie threatens Nikki that she better get her and her friend invited.<br /><br />The only solution Nikki can come up with is to join the newspaper to prevent Mackenzie from turning in Brandon for the prank. Nikki winds up off the sign-up list, but gets her the opportunity to write an anonymous advice column as Miss Know it All. Will Nikki be able to get closer to Brandon and prevent Mackenzie from turning Brandon in for a prank that was her fault?<br /><br />I've read enjoyed all of the books in this series. I love to read the little snippets that Briana, Nikki's sister, and Miss Penelope, a drawn-on face on Briana's hand. As I've mentioned in some of my other reviews, I would love to see a spin-off series just focused on them.<br /><br />I didn't love this one quite as much as the others, but this one was still pretty great. I wish there were moments of Nikki and Brandon in this one. This is a series that is a must read for younger girls and anybody that like reading fun contemporary middle grade books. Can't wait for the next installment. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11330803139317619928">Are you just dorkalicious? Well this is the book for you. Dork Diaries: Tales from a Not So Smart Miss-Know-It-All by Rachel Renee Russell is a Realistic Fiction book about Nikki Maxwell and her amazing private school adventures. Well, maybe not so amazing.<br/> Dork Diaries: Tales from a Not So Smart Miss-Know-It-All is about Nikki Maxwell, her enemy, Mackensie Hollister and her crush, Brandon Roberts. When Nikki and her best friends, Chloe and Zoe, decide to pull a devious prank on Mackensie, thing</span>
  <span id="freeText11330803139317619928" style="display:none">Are you just dorkalicious? Well this is the book for you. Dork Diaries: Tales from a Not So Smart Miss-Know-It-All by Rachel Renee Russell is a Realistic Fiction book about Nikki Maxwell and her amazing private school adventures. Well, maybe not so amazing.<br /> Dork Diaries: Tales from a Not So Smart Miss-Know-It-All is about Nikki Maxwell, her enemy, Mackensie Hollister and her crush, Brandon Roberts. When Nikki and her best friends, Chloe and Zoe, decide to pull a devious prank on Mackensie, things go a little too far. After all of the drama with the prank, Nikki thinks she could get a spot in the newspaper crew with her crush, Brandon, To straighten things out. Will Mackensie steal Brandon to herself? Will Nikki get a part in the newspaper crew? Read Dork Diaries: Tales from a Not So Smart Miss-Know-It-All to find out.<br /> I give this book five stars out of five stars. I like this book because I can really relate a lot of Nikki‚Äôs problems to my life problems. My favorite part is when Nikki finally gets to truly talk to Brandon. It is an amazing book for all ages. It can really show you how to appreciate the little things in life. But, before you read this one, you should read all the others in the series, such as: Book one Dork Diaries: Tales From a Not-So-Fabulous Life, Book 2 Dork Diaries: Tales From a Not-So-Popular Party Girl, Book 3 Dork Diaries: Tales From a Not-So-Talented Pop Star, Book 4 Dork Diaries: Tales From a Not so Graceful Ice Princess and this one is book 5. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText15891343928292397143" style="display:none"> Although I have read many books in 1st quarter, Dork diaries is my favorite. In Dork diaries-Tales from a Not-So-Smart-Miss-Know-It-All, Nikki wants to work as a reporter for the school but doesn't get the job. Instead, she becomes someone who answers peoples questions through a secret name. She learns that this job isn't as easy as she thought. She answers almost 200 questions a day! Talk about tiring. She is trying to keep Mackenzie from telling on her to the principle and do her job at the same time. Nikki's bully (Mackenzie) might be spreading rumors about her that Nikki doesn't know about. <br /><br /> Out of all the characters in the book, Nikki is my favorite. For example, she isn't afraid to express herself. She writes in her diary when people are around even when Mackenzie is next to her. It is the same with me and my Diabetes. Even when people are around, I am not afraid to express myself. Another reason Nikki is my favorite character is she has a little sibling to look after 24/7. Her little sisters name is Brianna. Brianna is annoying almost all the time but she also loving. I have a little brother named Jackson. He is sometimes annoying and is always loving and loves to share. I like Nikki as my favorite character because she isn't afraid to stand up for herself. <br /><br /> Out of all the books I have read, I would recommend this book to all 6th grade girls because Nikki is a 6th grader that is dealing with life just like us. She is a strong girl that is not afraid to express herself. This is a series book so there are 5 other books. The book is also funny. For example, Nikki was supposed to start exercising for a gym test that was coming up. She was supposed to do curl-ups but instead she thought it meant curling her hair. The second exercise she was supposed to do was push-ups but instead she thought it was the push up pops(ice cream). The third exercise she was supposed to do was pull-ups but instead she thought it was to pull on her socks every morning. The last exercise she was supposed to do was crunches but instead she thought it was to eat chips and listen to the sound of chips crack in her mouth.<br /><br /> </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2700654-brenda-kahn?shelf=wimp-appeal">wimp-appeal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2700654-brenda-kahn?shelf=school">school</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer472853860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1504946427497781512">As books with wimp appeal go, this one's pretty positive. While the author deftly captures tween perseveration, if I never hear something described as "super-" or see another OMG!!!!! again, I will die happy. And, I must admit that I'm getting tired of Nikki's fear of being exposed as a fraud. I feel as though I'm reading the same book over and over. My fifth graders can't get enough of them though and the fact that they're excited makes me happy.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('H/iQykUQVJrWWuLswp8DDMuEHazhVWVjr97HGkyCEWSzPCkCGYQ9p9ywyL/3ggP+yA445+c/gaNRVv4D+y4Y6g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
